Hope you guys are eagerly waiting for the most awaited festival, *Ganesh Chaturthi*.ğŸ’«
With the same exhilaration, we are going to make this festival more colourful and eco-friendly by setting up a stall where everyone are welcomed to buy eco-friendly ganesh idols made of clay. We request you to kindly fill the form. 
https://forms.gle/S6zSuRZP7hcLof8w7
ğŸ“Œ *Date:* 30/08/2022
ğŸ“Œ *Venue:* C-Block entrance

*Importance of clay idols:-*

In the Arabian Sea of  Mumbai coasts every year there are over *1.5 lakh* idols immersed leading to the fall of oxygen level in the sea by 50 percent right after the festival.

In order to eradicate the problem due to POP idols, clay idols are the best alternatives, as these dissolve in water easily and reduce water pollution to a greater extent.

As part of this awareness event, we are providing an amazing  opportunity to create your own *Ganesha Idol* and can also participate in *Best Idol Contest*. 

*Be the change, Go for Clay Ganesha*

Hello People!

Welcome to the world of AI.
Many functions constitute the human body and the nerve cell called "Neuron" is responsible for performing them. The study of neurons is called "Neuroscience". In AI, we call this _DEEP LEARNING_. We are back with another productive event- *DEEP LEARNING WORKSHOP.*

Deep Learning is a subfield of machine learning where complex algorithms are modelled to work in a way similar to humans. It enables a computer to perform complex functions like understanding human speech, automatically recognizing objects in images, etc. 

*DEEP LEARNING WORKSHOP* is a *3-day workshop* where you will get to know about deep learning basics and their implementation in python. â€œMachine learning is a prerequisite for deep learningâ€ is a myth. There are no prerequisites. 

*Note:*
â€¢	This workshop is open to all branches.
â€¢	Certificates will be issued to everyone with 75% attendance and a 60% score on the quiz. 
â€¢	All the resources will be shared at the end of the workshop. 
So, do join us in Neuro-World to witness the magic of deep learning to mimic humans!

*Date and Time:*
*31 Oct:* 10 am - 1 pm
*1st & 2nd Nov:* 10 am - 2:40 pm
*Venue:* KS Audi

Winter season has arrived. We are so lucky to have a shelter, food and can able to cover ourselves with blankets, sweaters.
But what about poor and homeless people???

There are millions of underprivileged who cannot afford even a blanket. They sleep in rags at footpath and roadside. They shiver due to cold breeze all the night and some old age persons die of these waves.

What can we do from our end?

Established in 2011, VOICE 4 Girls is an NGO that works with marginalised adolescent girls in India to re-imagine their identities, capabilities, and futures.
